\subsection{Detailed Description}
Author\-: Matthew Horridge\par
 The University Of Manchester\par
 Bio-\/\-Health Informatics Group Date\-: 24-\/\-Oct-\/2006 

Represents an O\-W\-L 2 \href{http://www.w3.org/TR/2009/REC-owl2-syntax-20091027/#Ontologies}{\tt Ontology} in the O\-W\-L 2 specification. 

An {\ttfamily \hyperlink{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_ontology}{O\-W\-L\-Ontology}} consists of a possibly empty set of \hyperlink{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_axiom}{org.\-semanticweb.\-owlapi.\-model.\-O\-W\-L\-Axiom}s and a possibly empty set of \hyperlink{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_annotation}{O\-W\-L\-Annotation}s. An ontology can have an ontology \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I} which can be used to identify the ontology. If it has an ontology \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I} then it may also have an ontology version \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I}. Since O\-W\-L 2, an ontology need not have an ontology \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I}. (See the \href{http://www.w3.org/TR/2009/REC-owl2-syntax-20091027/}{\tt O\-W\-L 2 Structural Specification}). 

An ontology cannot be modified directly. Changes must be applied via its {\ttfamily \hyperlink{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_ontology_manager}{O\-W\-L\-Ontology\-Manager}}.

Determines if the signature of this ontology, or possibly the signature of one of the ontologies in the imports closure of this ontology, contains an \hyperlink{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_annotation_property}{O\-W\-L\-Annotation\-Property} that has the specified \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I}. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em owl\-Annotation\-Property\-I\-R\-I} & The \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I} of the \hyperlink{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_annotation_property}{O\-W\-L\-Annotation\-Property} to check for \\
\hline
{\em include\-Imports\-Closure} & {\ttfamily true} if the signature of the ontologies in the imports closure of this ontology should be checked, {\ttfamily false} if just the signature of this ontology should be chekced. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
If {\ttfamily include\-Imports\-Closure=true} then returns {\ttfamily true} if there is an \hyperlink{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_annotation_property}{O\-W\-L\-Annotation\-Property} with {\ttfamily owl\-Annotation\-Property\-I\-R\-I} as its \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I} in the signature of at least one ontology in the imports clousre of this ontology and {\ttfamily false} if this is not the case. If {\ttfamily include\-Imports\-Closure=false} then returns {\ttfamily true} if the signature of this ontology contains an \hyperlink{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_annotation_property}{O\-W\-L\-Annotation\-Property} that has {\ttfamily owl\-Annotation\-Property\-I\-R\-I} as its \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I} and {\ttfamily false} if the signature of this ontology does not contain a class with {\ttfamily owl\-Annotation\-Property\-I\-R\-I} as its \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I}. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

)}}\label{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_ontology_adda4d6ea7571709ae0e324538a02b204}
Determines if this ontology contains the specified axiom, but ignoring any annotations on this axiom. For example, if the ontology contains {\ttfamily Sub\-Class\-Of(Annotation(p V) A B)} then this method will return {\ttfamily true} if the ontology contains {\ttfamily Sub\-Class\-Of(\-A B)} or {\ttfamily Sub\-Class\-Of(Annotation(q S) A B)} for any annotation property {\ttfamily q} and any annotation value {\ttfamily S}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em axiom} & The axiom to test for. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
{\ttfamily true} if this ontology contains this axiom with or without annotations. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Determines if the signature of this ontology, and possibly the signature of any of the ontologies in the imports closure of this ontology, contains the specified entity.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em owl\-Entity} & The entity \\
\hline
{\em include\-Imports\-Closure} & Specifies whether the imports closure should be examined for the entity reference or not. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
{\ttfamily true} if the ontology contains a reference to the specified entity, otherwise {\ttfamily false} The set that is returned is a copy -\/ it will not be updated if the ontology changes. It is therefore safe to apply changes to this ontology while iterating over this set. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Determines if the signature of this ontology and possibly its imports closure contains a class, object property, data property, named individual, annotation property or datatype with the specified \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I}. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
If {\ttfamily include\-Imports\-Closure=true} then returns {\ttfamily true} if the signature of this ontology or the signature of an ontology in the imports closure of this ontology contains a class, object property, data property, named individual, annotation property or datatype with the specified \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_i_r_i}{I\-R\-I}. \begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A set of annotations on this ontology. The set returned will be a copy -\/ modifying the set will have no effect on the annotations in this ontology, similarly, any changes that affect the annotations on this ontology will not change the returned set. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\hypertarget{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_ontology_a650a728c2c12af706c91914d82bed2a1}{\index{org\-::semanticweb\-::owlapi\-::model\-::\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology@{org\-::semanticweb\-::owlapi\-::model\-::\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology}!get\-Axioms@{get\-Axioms}}
\index{get\-Axioms@{get\-Axioms}!org::semanticweb::owlapi::model::OWLOntology@{org\-::semanticweb\-::owlapi\-::model\-::\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology}}
\subsubsection[{get\-Axioms}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}Set$<${\bf O\-W\-L\-Axiom}$>$ org.\-semanticweb.\-owlapi.\-model.\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology.\-get\-Axioms (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
{}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_ontology_a650a728c2c12af706c91914d82bed2a1}
Retrieves all of the axioms in this ontology. Note that to test whether or not this ontology is empty (i.\-e. contains no axioms, the is\-Empty method is preferred over \hyperlink{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_ontology_a650a728c2c12af706c91914d82bed2a1}{get\-Axioms()}.\hyperlink{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_ontology_ab318bb166cbf65aca5dccbdbaa7298c6}{is\-Empty()}. )

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The set of all axioms in this ontology, including logical axioms and annotation axioms. The set that is returned is a copy of the axioms in the ontology -\/ it will not be updated if the ontology changes. It is recommended that the {\ttfamily contains\-Axiom} method is used to determine whether or not this ontology contains a particular axiom rather than using \hyperlink{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_ontology_a650a728c2c12af706c91914d82bed2a1}{get\-Axioms()}.contains(). 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\hypertarget{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_ontology_af95c5f071089ae80cc2d105153ef384f}{\index{org\-::semanticweb\-::owlapi\-::model\-::\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology@{org\-::semanticweb\-::owlapi\-::model\-::\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology}!get\-Axioms@{get\-Axioms}}

\subsubsection[{get\-Axioms}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}Set$<${\bf O\-W\-L\-Class\-Axiom}$>$ org.\-semanticweb.\-owlapi.\-model.\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology.\-get\-Axioms (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf O\-W\-L\-Class}}]{cls}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_ontology_af95c5f071089ae80cc2d105153ef384f}
Gets the axioms that form the definition/description of a class.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em cls} & The class whose describing axioms are to be retrieved. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A set of class axioms that describe the class. This set includes 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Subclass axioms where the subclass is equal to the specified class  
\item Equivalent class axioms where the specified class is an operand in the equivalent class axiom 
\item Disjoint class axioms where the specified class is an operand in the disjoint class axiom 
\item Disjoint union axioms, where the specified class is the named class that is equivalent to the disjoint union 
\end{DoxyItemize}The set that is returned is a copy -\/ it will not be updated if the ontology changes. It is therefore safe to apply changes to this ontology while iterating over this set. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\hypertarget{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_ontology_a529d12aabbf714c8535961b96294677a}{\index{org\-::semanticweb\-::owlapi\-::model\-::\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology@{org\-::semanticweb\-::owlapi\-::model\-::\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology}!get\-Axioms@{get\-Axioms}}
\index{get\-Axioms@{get\-Axioms}!org::semanticweb::owlapi::model::OWLOntology@{org\-::semanticweb\-::owlapi\-::model\-::\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology}}
\subsubsection[{get\-Axioms}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}Set$<${\bf O\-W\-L\-Object\-Property\-Axiom}$>$ org.\-semanticweb.\-owlapi.\-model.\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology.\-get\-Axioms (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf O\-W\-L\-Object\-Property\-Expression}}]{prop}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_ontology_a529d12aabbf714c8535961b96294677a}
Gets the axioms that form the definition/description of an object property.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em prop} & The property whose defining axioms are to be retrieved. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A set of object property axioms that includes 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Sub-\/property axioms where the sub property is equal to the specified property 
\item Equivalent property axioms where the axiom contains the specified property 
\item Equivalent property axioms that contain the inverse of the specified property 
\item Disjoint property axioms that contain the specified property 
\item Domain axioms that specify a domain of the specified property 
\item Range axioms that specify a range of the specified property 
\item Any property characteristic axiom (i.\-e. Functional, Symmetric, Reflexive etc.) whose subject is the specified property 
\item Inverse properties axioms that contain the specified property 
\end{DoxyItemize}The set that is returned is a copy -\/ it will not be updated if the ontology changes. It is therefore safe to apply changes to this ontology while iterating over this set. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Gets the set of axioms contained in this ontology that have the same \char`\"{}logical structure\char`\"{} as the specified axiom.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em axiom} & The axiom that specifies the logical structure of the axioms to retrieve. If this axiom is annotated then the annotations are ignored. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A set of axioms such that for any two axioms, {\ttfamily axiom\-A} and {\ttfamily axiom\-B} in the set, {\ttfamily axiom\-A.\-get\-Axiom\-Without\-Annotations()} is equal to {\ttfamily axiom\-B.\-get\-Axiom\-Without\-Annotations()}. The specified axiom will be contained in the set. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Gets the datatypes that are in the signature of this ontology, and possibly the imports closure of this ontology. \begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See Also}
\hyperlink{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_ontology_aee70ef186c308d4a41df64199ced2e2c}{get\-Signature()} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em include\-Imports\-Closure} & Specifies whether datatypes should be drawn from the signature of just this ontology or the imports closure of this ontology. If {\ttfamily true} then the set of datatypes returned will correspond to the union of the datatypes in the signatures of the ontologies in the imports closure of this ontology. If {\ttfamily false} then the set of datatypes returned will correspond to the datatypes that are in the signature of this just this ontology. \\

\end{DoxyParams}

The set that is returned is a copy -\/ it will not be updated if the ontology changes. It is therefore safe to apply changes to this ontology while iterating over this set. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\hypertarget{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_ontology_a2e1ae99aa7e9b9d2bfae42e1348747e4}{\index{org\-::semanticweb\-::owlapi\-::model\-::\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology@{org\-::semanticweb\-::owlapi\-::model\-::\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology}!get\-Direct\-Imports@{get\-Direct\-Imports}}
\index{get\-Direct\-Imports@{get\-Direct\-Imports}!org::semanticweb::owlapi::model::OWLOntology@{org\-::semanticweb\-::owlapi\-::model\-::\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology}}
\subsubsection[{get\-Direct\-Imports}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}Set$<${\bf O\-W\-L\-Ontology}$>$ org.\-semanticweb.\-owlapi.\-model.\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology.\-get\-Direct\-Imports (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
{}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
) throws {\bf Unknown\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology\-Exception}}}\label{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_ontology_a2e1ae99aa7e9b9d2bfae42e1348747e4}
Gets the set of {\itshape loaded} ontologies that this ontology is related to via the directly\-Imports relation. See Section 3.\-4 of the O\-W\-L 2 specification for the definition of the directly\-Imports relation. 

Note that there may be fewer ontologies in the set returned by this method than there are I\-R\-Is in the set returned by the \hyperlink{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_ontology_a9b78b53552c9c1f71709f9c893388e81}{get\-Direct\-Imports\-Documents()} method. This will be the case if some of the ontologies that are directly imported by this ontology are not loaded for what ever reason. 

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A set of ontologies such that for this ontology O, and each ontology O' in the set, (O, O') is in the directly\-Imports relation.
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\em \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_unknown_o_w_l_ontology_exception}{Unknown\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology\-Exception}} & If this ontology is no longer managed by its manager because it was removed from the manager. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyExceptions}

Gets the set of disjoint class axioms that contain the specified class as an operand.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\end{DoxyReturn}

Gets the set of disjoint union axioms that have the specified class as the named class that is equivalent to the disjoint union of operands. For example, if the ontology contained the axiom Disjoint\-Union(A, prop\-P some C, D, E) this axiom would be returned for class A (but not for D or E).


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em owl\-Class} & The class that indexes the axioms to be retrieved. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The set that is returned is a copy -\/ it will not be updated if the ontology changes. It is therefore safe to apply changes to this ontology while iterating over this set. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{get\-General\-Class\-Axioms@{get\-General\-Class\-Axioms}!org::semanticweb::owlapi::model::OWLOntology@{org\-::semanticweb\-::owlapi\-::model\-::\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology}}

\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_ontology_ae40508c509dccec32fb78b4b8cfafab4}
Gets the set of general axioms in this ontology. This includes\-: 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Subclass axioms that have a complex class as the subclass 
\item Equivalent class axioms that don't contain any named classes ({\ttfamily \hyperlink{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_class}{O\-W\-L\-Class}}es) 
\item Disjoint class axioms that don't contain any named classes ({\ttfamily \hyperlink{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_class}{O\-W\-L\-Class}}es) 
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The set that is returned is a copy of the axioms in the ontology -\/ it will not be updated if the ontology changes. It is therefore safe to apply changes to this ontology while iterating over this set. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\hypertarget{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_ontology_a494f984a2879a4b943ee3e342064fd89}{\index{org\-::semanticweb\-::owlapi\-::model\-::\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology@{org\-::semanticweb\-::owlapi\-::model\-::\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology}!get\-Imports@{get\-Imports}}
\index{get\-Imports@{get\-Imports}!org::semanticweb::owlapi::model::OWLOntology@{org\-::semanticweb\-::owlapi\-::model\-::\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology}}
\subsubsection[{get\-Imports}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}Set$<${\bf O\-W\-L\-Ontology}$>$ org.\-semanticweb.\-owlapi.\-model.\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology.\-get\-Imports (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
{}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
) throws {\bf Unknown\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology\-Exception}}}\label{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_ontology_a494f984a2879a4b943ee3e342064fd89}
Gets the set of {\itshape loaded} ontologies that this ontology is related to via the {\itshape transitive closure} of the \href{http://www.w3.org/TR/2009/REC-owl2-syntax-20091027/#Imports}{\tt directly\-Imports relation}. 

For example, if this ontology imports ontology B, and ontology B imports ontology C, then this method will return the set consisting of ontology B and ontology C. 

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The set of ontologies that this ontology is related to via the transitive closure of the directly\-Imports relation. The set that is returned is a copy -\/ it will not be updated if the ontology changes. It is therefore safe to apply changes to this ontology while iterating over this set.
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyExceptions}{Exceptions}
{\em \hyperlink{classorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_unknown_o_w_l_ontology_exception}{Unknown\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology\-Exception}} & if this ontology is no longer managed by its manager because it was removed from the manager. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyExceptions}

\hypertarget{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_ontology_a0498eba3a4ae9f428b85a629e0263a8f}{\index{org\-::semanticweb\-::owlapi\-::model\-::\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology@{org\-::semanticweb\-::owlapi\-::model\-::\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology}!get\-Imports\-Closure@{get\-Imports\-Closure}}
\index{get\-Imports\-Closure@{get\-Imports\-Closure}!org::semanticweb::owlapi::model::OWLOntology@{org\-::semanticweb\-::owlapi\-::model\-::\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology}}
\subsubsection[{get\-Imports\-Closure}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}Set$<${\bf O\-W\-L\-Ontology}$>$ org.\-semanticweb.\-owlapi.\-model.\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology.\-get\-Imports\-Closure (

Gets the set of {\itshape loaded} ontologies that this ontology is related to via the {\itshape reflexive transitive closure} of the directly\-Imports relation as defined in Section 3.\-4 of the O\-W\-L 2 Structural Specification. (i.\-e. The set returned includes all ontologies returned by the \hyperlink{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_ontology_a494f984a2879a4b943ee3e342064fd89}{get\-Imports()} method plus this ontology.)

For example, if this ontology imports ontology B, and ontology B imports ontology C, then this method will return the set consisting of this ontology, ontology B and ontology C. 

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The set of ontologies in the reflexive transitive closure of the directly\-Imports relation.
\end{DoxyReturn}

\hline
\end{DoxyExceptions}

Gets the individuals that are in the signature of this ontology, and possibly the imports closure of this ontology. \begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See Also}
\hyperlink{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_ontology_aee70ef186c308d4a41df64199ced2e2c}{get\-Signature()} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em include\-Imports\-Closure} & Specifies whether individuals should be drawn from the signature of just this ontology or the imports closure of this ontology. If {\ttfamily true} then the set of individuals returned will correspond to the union of the individuals in the signatures of the ontologies in the imports closure of this ontology. If {\ttfamily false} then the set of individuals returned will correspond to the individuals that are in the signature of this just this ontology. \\

Gets all of the axioms in the ontology that affect the logical meaning of the ontology. In other words, this method returns all axioms that are not annotation axioms, or declaration axioms.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A set of axioms which are of the type {\ttfamily \hyperlink{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_logical_axiom}{O\-W\-L\-Logical\-Axiom}} The set that is returned is a copy of the axioms in the ontology -\/ it will not be updated if the ontology changes. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Gets the object properties that are in the signature of this ontology, and possibly the imports closure of this ontology.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em include\-Imports\-Closure} & Specifies whether object properties should be drawn from the signature of just this ontology or the imports closure of this ontology. If {\ttfamily true} then the set of object properties returned will correspond to the union of the object properties in the signatures of the ontologies in the imports closure of this ontology. If {\ttfamily false} then the set of object properties returned will correspond to the object properties that are in the signature of this just this ontology. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A set of object properties that are in the signature of this ontology and possibly the union of the signatures of the ontologies in the imports closure of this ontology. The set that is returned is a copy -\/ it will not be updated if the ontology changes. It is therefore safe to apply changes to this ontology while iterating over this set. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\hypertarget{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_ontology_aee70ef186c308d4a41df64199ced2e2c}{\index{org\-::semanticweb\-::owlapi\-::model\-::\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology@{org\-::semanticweb\-::owlapi\-::model\-::\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology}!get\-Signature@{get\-Signature}}
\index{get\-Signature@{get\-Signature}!org::semanticweb::owlapi::model::OWLOntology@{org\-::semanticweb\-::owlapi\-::model\-::\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology}}
\subsubsection[{get\-Signature}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}Set$<${\bf O\-W\-L\-Entity}$>$ org.\-semanticweb.\-owlapi.\-model.\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology.\-get\-Signature (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
{}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_ontology_aee70ef186c308d4a41df64199ced2e2c}
Gets the entities that are in the signature of this ontology. The signature of an ontology is the set of entities that are used to build axioms and annotations in the ontology. (See \href{http://www.w3.org/TR/2009/REC-owl2-syntax-20091027/#Entities.2C_Literals.2C_and_Anonymous_Individuals}{\tt The O\-W\-L 2 Structural Specification})

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A set of {\ttfamily \hyperlink{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_entity}{O\-W\-L\-Entity}} objects. The set that is returned is a copy -\/ it will not be updated if the ontology changes. It is therefore safe to apply changes to this ontology while iterating over this set. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\hypertarget{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_ontology_a86133864a3dc50b9ad7be0093aef6b9c}{\index{org\-::semanticweb\-::owlapi\-::model\-::\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology@{org\-::semanticweb\-::owlapi\-::model\-::\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology}!get\-Signature@{get\-Signature}}
\index{get\-Signature@{get\-Signature}!org::semanticweb::owlapi::model::OWLOntology@{org\-::semanticweb\-::owlapi\-::model\-::\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology}}
\subsubsection[{get\-Signature}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}Set$<${\bf O\-W\-L\-Entity}$>$ org.\-semanticweb.\-owlapi.\-model.\-O\-W\-L\-Ontology.\-get\-Signature (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{boolean}]{include\-Imports\-Closure}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_ontology_a86133864a3dc50b9ad7be0093aef6b9c}
Gets the entities that are in the signature of this ontology. The signature of an ontology is the set of entities that are used to build axioms and annotations in the ontology. (See \href{http://www.w3.org/TR/2009/REC-owl2-syntax-20091027/#Entities.2C_Literals.2C_and_Anonymous_Individuals}{\tt The O\-W\-L 2 Structural Specification})


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em include\-Imports\-Closure} & Specifies whether or not the returned set of entities should represent the signature of just this ontology, or the signature of the imports closure of this ontology. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A set of {\ttfamily \hyperlink{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_entity}{O\-W\-L\-Entity}} objects. The set that is returned is a copy -\/ it will not be updated if the ontology changes. It is therefore safe to apply changes to this ontology while iterating over this set. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See Also}
\hyperlink{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_ontology_a1f6340caef27fd1791a31603940f7549}{get\-Classes\-In\-Signature()}

\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_ontology_ab318bb166cbf65aca5dccbdbaa7298c6}
Determines if this ontology is empty -\/ an ontology is empty if it does not contain any axioms (i.\-e. \hyperlink{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_ontology_a650a728c2c12af706c91914d82bed2a1}{get\-Axioms()} returns the empty set), and it does not have any annotations (i.\-e. \hyperlink{interfaceorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1model_1_1_o_w_l_ontology_a47069e02d864e875ac338bb29df82ab4}{get\-Annotations()} returns the empty set).

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
{\ttfamily true} if the ontology is empty, otherwise {\ttfamily false}. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
